Yunjincheng Mansion is on West Street, just a few steps away from the famous Rishengchang. It is said that this was the home of the Yin brothers two or three hundred years ago. They ran a pharmacy and other businesses on the same street. They should have met Boss Lei from Rishengchang and Boss Mao from Wei Taihou, right? .
Although the house has been redesigned and restored, traces of its history can still be seen everywhere. The lobby managers are very happy to explain the story behind the building to the guests who are staying. Listening to it, you will be very grateful for your decision. When you visit Pingyao, you must have such an experience of staying in history.
Although it was the weather in early March, the room was very warm even without the heating on. The furniture was decorated in an old style, and even the latches on the cabinets were very unique. Whether it is the manager at the lobby or Xiaoning Guanjia, who added WeChat early, the service attitude is very warm and considerate. It was my mother's birthday during our stay, and the lobby manager gave us two bowls of longevity noodles for free!
If you have good legs and feet, it is very convenient to stay in an inn in a pedestrian street like Yunjincheng. Many scenic spots are not far nearby, and you can reach them in minutes with a quick step. However, living here is a little inconvenient for the elderly with weak legs and feet, because some scenic spots have to go up and down stairs, and some roads are a bit muddy and uneven. It is not convenient for a wheelchair to go around. The peripheral sightseeing cars are blocked outside the fence and cannot be directed. superior. Fortunately, we had already taken the sightseeing bus to see all the main attractions. After moving to Yunjincheng, we were left with Zhenguo Temple and Shuanglin Temple. Yunjincheng Mansion can rent out wheelchairs. I only need to use the wheelchair to push the old man outside the lower west gate or north gate, and then meet up with the taxi driver. The old man is basically not tired. When we left Pingyao, Master Xiao Xue from the residence helped us carry our big and small bags and took us to the train station entrance. The service was very patient and attentive.
All in all, it was a great experience staying at Yunjincheng. Ctrip‚Äôs group purchase prices are great value for money. Travelers who prefer to experience Pingyao's history in depth rather than just looking at it briefly should definitely experience it if their budget allows!

On one side of the street is the hotel reception + guest rooms, and on the other side is the hotel's own cafe + guest rooms. Yunjincheng Mansion should be the most upscale and heroic in the ancient city. The coffee in the cafe is pretty good.
Service: Very caring, especially the young man at the front desk, who is very enthusiastic. He arranges the pick-up and drop-off. As long as there is any problem, he will come to help you solve it as soon as you call.
Before leaving, the hotel manager also sent a bottle of their own mature vinegar, which was a very pleasant stay.
